< Review>
Do not recommend to bring your young kid to this one. My son got a bee sting and started to have an allergic reaction. We bought him there because it is close enough. Whoever saw him first say would give him a shot and came back and said they did not have that small dose for his age. So they sent us to CVS to get the liquid instead. After taking the dose that was recommended by the doc, my son got worse and started to have trouble of breathing. We immediately took him to ER. The ER doctor told us he was confused by the dose that was given by the previous urgent care doc, it was common sense to know the dose and how come my son was given that little.

If you do not know what to do, PLEASE inform us to take him to ER, rather than sending us home and let my 21 months suffer for two and half hours more. My son got his shot at ER and after 20 mins he felt better. The ER doctor double confirmed with me twice about the dose and he wrote a new dose for my son. And he is fine now.

< Review>
I initially went there for a TB test, which was quick and cheap.  $5 if I recall.

If they cover your insurance, then this is a great place to get urgent care.  Only problem is they're not open 24/7, but their hours are still pretty good.  I find the receptionists to be cold sometimes (as is usually the case at many medical practices), but once you get past them, it's like you've entered a magical land of amazingly friendly, professional, knowledeable and polite medical staff.

The 2nd time I went in, I had my elbow checked out after falling on it snowboarding.  The medical aide and doctor were quick, friendly, polite, and professional.  I was concerned I might have a hairline fracture so an X-ray was done quickly without a fuss.  I was in and out in less than 30 min!  Like fast food medical care, but at high quality.  However, I'm guessing they might be expensive if you don't have insurance.  The doctor also followed up with me 1 week later!  I was impressed!</Review>

Oh my goodness. Look no further! This is your nail salon. I was visiting from Salt lake City. Noticed a was in desperate need of a new full set. Stumbled upon this salon. Boy am I grateful that I did. From the moment I walked in the door...I felt welcomed. Ben was my manicurist and Lana, his wife, waxed my eyebrows. Truly, salt of the Earth kind of people. < text>
During SF quarantine, I found myself stuck on foot in Santa Clata. I did some urban hiking and ended up at Hotel Rose Garden. The night manager, Sanjit, was so patient,  helpful, professional, and kind. The non-smoking king bed room I stayed in for the night had a sparkling clean bathroom (and bathtub), plenty of channels to surf, and very comfortable pillows. Wifi is zippy  and works in the rooms and outside. The property is very well-kept and all the room doors face the inside courtyard, so it feels much safer. The pricing is highly competitive for the area and there's easy access to the highway. If you are craving good eats, check out Wicked Chicken near Safeway.

Had a very pleasant stay after a stressful day. Definitely will check in again when in the area.<//text>

The walls are paper thin in the hotel and we could hear the unpleasant conversation that was not for the young ears of my two daughters from the room next door.
